Page 463 

019926,003493:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019927,003494: 
019928,003495:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019929,003496:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019930,003497:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019931,003498:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019932,003499: 
019933,003500:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019934,003501:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019935,003502:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019936,003503:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019937,003504:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019938,003505:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019939,003506:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019940,003507: 
019941,003508:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019942,003509:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019943,003510:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019944,003511:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019945,003512:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019946,003513: 
019947,003514:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019948,003515:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019949,003516:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019950,003517:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019951,003518:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019952,003519: 
019953,003520:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019954,003521:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019955,003522:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019956,003523: 
019957,003524: 
019958,003525:                                                                                                  #  .
019959,003526: 
019960,003527:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019961,003528:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019962,003529:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019963,003530:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019964,003531: 
019965,003532:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019966,003533:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019967,003534:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019968,003535:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019969,003536:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019970,003537:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019972,003539:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019973,003540: 
019974,003541:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019975,003542:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019976,003543:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019977,003544:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019978,003545:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019979,003546:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019980,003547: 
019981,003548:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019982,003549:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019983,003550: 
019984,003551: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019985,003552: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019986,003553: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019987,003554: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019988,003555: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019989,003556: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019990,003557: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019991,003558: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019992,003559: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019993,003560: 
019994,003561:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019995,003562:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019996,003563:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019997,003564:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019998,003565:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019999,003566: 
020000,003567:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
020001,003568:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020002,003569:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020003,003570:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
020004,003571:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020005,003572:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020006,003573:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
020007,003574:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020008,003575:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
020009,003576:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
020010,003577:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
020011,003578:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
020012,003579:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
020013,003580: 
020014,003581:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
020015,003582:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
020016,003583:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
020017,003584: 
020018,003585:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
020019,003586:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
020020,003587:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

020022,003589:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
020023,003590:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
020024,003591:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020025,003592:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
020026,003593:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
020027,003594:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY

020162,003729:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
020163,003730:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020164,003731:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020165,003732:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020166,003733:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020167,003734:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020168,003735:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
